NOTE: PROCEDURE PRINTTO used (Total process time):

      cpu time            0.00 seconds

304  RUN;

NOTE: PROCEDURE MEANS used (Total process time):
      real time           0.01 seconds
      cpu time            0.01 seconds
      

305  
306  * Label new school mean variables;
307  DATA work.SchoolMeans; SET work.SchoolMeans;
308       Nperschool = _FREQ_; * Saving N per school;
309       DROP _TYPE_ _FREQ_;  * Dropping unneeded SAS-created variables;
310       LABEL Nperschool= "Nperschool: # Students Contributing Data"
311             SMfrlunch=  "SMfrlunch: School Mean 0=No, 1=Free/Reduced Lunch"
312             SMmath=     "SMmath: School Mean Math Outcome";
313       * Center school mean predictor;
314       SMfrlunch30 = SMfrlunch - .30;
315       LABEL SMfrlunch30= "SMfrlunch30: 0=.30)";
316  RUN;

NOTE: There were 381 observations read from the data set WORK.SCHOOLMEANS.
NOTE: The data set WORK.SCHOOLMEANS has 381 observations and 5 variables.
NOTE: DATA statement used (Total process time):
      real time           0.00 seconds
      cpu time            0.00 seconds
      

317  
318  * Merge school means back with individual data;
319  DATA work.grade10; MERGE work.grade10 work.SchoolMeans; BY schoolID;
320       * Arbitrarily selecting only schools with at least 30 students;
321       IF Nperschool < 31 THEN DELETE;
322  RUN;

388  
389  TITLE "SAS Model 6: Add Level-2 Interaction of Quadratic School Free/Reduced Lunch";
390  PROC MIXED DATA=work.grade10 NOCLPRINT COVTEST NAMELEN=100 IC METHOD=REML;
391       CLASS schoolID studentID;
392       MODEL math = frlunch SMfrlunch30 frlunch*SMfrlunch30 SMfrlunch30*SMfrlunch30
393                     / SOLUTION DDFM=Satterthwaite OUTPM=work.PredTotal;
394       RANDOM INTERCEPT frlunch / G TYPE=UN SUBJECT=schoolID;
395       ODS OUTPUT CovParms=CovInt2 InfoCrit=FitInt2;
396       CONTRAST "Test of Omnibus FR Lunch Interaction" frlunch*SMfrlunch30 1, SMfrlunch30*SMfrlunch30 1;
397       ESTIMATE "FR Lunch Between-School Simple Main Effect"  frlunch 1 SMfrlunch30 1;
398       ESTIMATE "FR Lunch Between-School Interaction"  frlunch*SMfrlunch30 1 SMfrlunch30*SMfrlunch30 1;
399  RUN;

275  RUN;

NOTE: There were 15826 observations read from the data set WORK.GRADE10.
NOTE: The data set WORK.SCHOOLMEANS has 381 observations and 5 variables.

      real time           0.01 seconds
      cpu time            0.01 seconds
      

276  
277  * Label new school mean variables;
278  DATA work.SchoolMeans; SET work.SchoolMeans;
279       Nperschool = _FREQ_; * Saving N per school;
280       DROP _TYPE_ _FREQ_;  * Dropping unneeded SAS-created variables;
281       LABEL Nperschool= "Nperschool: # Students Contributing Data"
282             SMfrlunch=  "SMfrlunch: School Mean 0=No, 1=Free/Reduced Lunch"
283             SMmath=     "SMmath: School Mean Math Outcome";
284       * Center school mean predictor;
285       SMfrlunch30 = SMfrlunch - .30;
286       LABEL SMfrlunch30= "SMfrlunch30: 0=.30)";
287  RUN;

NOTE: There were 381 observations read from the data set WORK.SCHOOLMEANS.
NOTE: The data set WORK.SCHOOLMEANS has 381 observations and 5 variables.
NOTE: DATA statement used (Total process time):
      real time           0.00 seconds
      cpu time            0.00 seconds
      

288  
289  * Merge school means back with individual data;
290  DATA work.grade10; MERGE work.grade10 work.SchoolMeans; BY schoolID;
291       * Arbitrarily selecting only schools with at least 30 students;
292       IF Nperschool < 31 THEN DELETE;
293  RUN;

311  
312  TITLE "SAS Model 1: 2-Level Empty Means, Random Intercept for Math Outcome";
313  PROC MIXED DATA=work.grade10 NOCLPRINT COVTEST NAMELEN=100 IC METHOD=REML;
314       CLASS schoolID; * Put nesting variable on CLASS to speed estimation;
315       MODEL math = / SOLUTION DDFM=Satterthwaite OUTPM=PredEmpty;
316       * Asking for G for all, V and VCORR for first school in order of schoolID;
317       RANDOM INTERCEPT / G V=1 VCORR=1 TYPE=UN SUBJECT=schoolID; * VCORR gives ICC;
318       * Asking for R for first school in order of schoolID;
319       REPEATED / R=1 TYPE=VC SUBJECT=schoolID;  * Default R matrix is diagonal (VC);
320       * ODS saves results for pseudo-R2 macro;
321       ODS OUTPUT CovParms=CovEmpty; RUN; TITLE;

348  TITLE "SAS Model 4: Add Random Effect of Student Free/Reduced Lunch";
349  PROC MIXED DATA=work.grade10 NOCLPRINT COVTEST NAMELEN=100 IC METHOD=REML;
350       CLASS schoolID;
351       MODEL math = frlunch SMfrlunch30 / SOLUTION DDFM=Satterthwaite;
352       * Asking for G and GCORR for all, V and VCORR for first school in order of schoolID;
353       RANDOM INTERCEPT frlunch / G GCORR V=1 VCORR=1 TYPE=UN SUBJECT=schoolID;
354       * Asking for R for first school in order of schoolID;
355       REPEATED / R=1 TYPE=VC SUBJECT=schoolID;  * Default R matrix is diagonal (VC);
356       ODS OUTPUT CovParms=CovFR2RandFR1 InfoCrit=FitFR2RandFR1; RUN; TITLE;

370  TITLE "SAS Model 6: Add Level-2 Interaction of Quadratic School Free/Reduced Lunch";
371  PROC MIXED DATA=work.grade10 NOCLPRINT COVTEST NAMELEN=100 IC METHOD=REML;
372       CLASS schoolID;
373       MODEL math = frlunch SMfrlunch30 frlunch*SMfrlunch30 SMfrlunch30*SMfrlunch30
374                     / SOLUTION DDFM=Satterthwaite OUTPM=work.PredTotal;
375       RANDOM INTERCEPT frlunch / G TYPE=UN SUBJECT=schoolID;
376       ODS OUTPUT CovParms=CovInt2 InfoCrit=FitInt2;
377       CONTRAST "Test of Omnibus FR Lunch Interaction" frlunch*SMfrlunch30 1, SMfrlunch30*SMfrlunch30 1;
378       ESTIMATE "FR Lunch Between-School Simple Main Effect"  frlunch 1 SMfrlunch30 1;
379       ESTIMATE "FR Lunch Between-School Interaction"  frlunch*SMfrlunch30 1 SMfrlunch30*SMfrlunch30 1;
380  RUN;

136  TITLE "SAS Model 1: 2-Level Empty Means, Random Intercept for Math Outcome";
137  PROC MIXED DATA=work.grade10 NOCLPRINT COVTEST NAMELEN=100 IC METHOD=REML;
138       CLASS schoolID; * Put nesting variable on CLASS to speed estimation;
139       MODEL math = / SOLUTION DDFM=Satterthwaite OUTPM=PredEmpty;
140       * Asking for G for all, V and VCORR for first school in order of schoolID;
141       RANDOM INTERCEPT / G V=1 VCORR=1 TYPE=UN SUBJECT=schoolID; * VCORR gives ICC;
142       * Asking for R for first school in order of schoolID;
143       REPEATED / R=1 TYPE=VC SUBJECT=schoolID;  * Default R matrix is diagonal (VC);
144       * ODS saves results for pseudo-R2 macro;
145       ODS OUTPUT CovParms=CovEmpty; RUN; TITLE;

441!      TITLE;

442  * Output options: all can be turned on/off by adding or removing the NO;
443  * page number, date, centering, or page breaks, page length and width;
444    OPTIONS NOnumber NOdate NOcenter FormDlim=' ' PageSize=MAX LineSize=MAX;
445  * Open datasets even if the formats are not available;
446    OPTIONS NOfmterr;
447  * Eliminate SAS default titles and names of tables in output (TRACE ON to show);
448    TITLE; ODS TRACE OFF;
449  * Turn on old-school output in addition to HTML output;
450    ODS LISTING;
451  
452  ***********************************************************************************;
453  *******     MACRO PROGRAMS TO AUTOMATE CALCULATIONS FOR THIS EXAMPLE        *******;
454  *******               NOTHING IN HERE NEEDS TO BE CHANGED                   *******;
455  ***********************************************************************************;
456  
457  * To use TotalR2 macro;
458  * DV =        Case-sensitive name of dependent variable;
459  * PredFewer = Name of OUTPM= data file of predicted outcomes for nested model;
460  * PredMore =  Name of OUTPM= data file of predicted outcomes for comparison model;
461  %MACRO TotalR2(DV, PredFewer, PredMore);
462  PROC CORR NOPRINT NOSIMPLE DATA=&PredFewer. OUTP=CorrFewer; VAR pred &DV.; RUN;
463  PROC CORR NOPRINT NOSIMPLE DATA=&PredMore.  OUTP=CorrMore;  VAR pred &DV.; RUN;
464  DATA CorrFewer; LENGTH Name $30.; SET CorrFewer; Name="&PredFewer."; RUN;
465  DATA CorrMore;  LENGTH Name $30.; SET CorrMore;  Name="&PredMore.";  RUN;
466  DATA CorrCompare; LENGTH Name $30.; SET CorrFewer CorrMore;
467       IF Pred=. THEN Pred=0;
468       PredCorr=Pred; TotalR2=PredCorr*PredCorr;
469       IF _NAME_="Pred" OR MISSING(_NAME_)=1 THEN DELETE; DROP Pred; RUN;
470  DATA CorrCompare; SET CorrCompare; TotalR2Diff=TotalR2-LAG1(TotalR2);
471       KEEP Name PredCorr TotalR2 TotalR2Diff; RUN;
472  TITLE2 "Total R2 (% Reduction) for &PredFewer. vs. &PredMore.";
473  PROC PRINT NOOBS DATA=CorrCompare; RUN; TITLE2;
474  %MEND TotalR2;
475  
476  * To use PseudoR2 macro;
477  * Ncov =     TOTAL # entries in covariance parameter estimates table;
478  * CovFewer = Name of ODS CovParms table for nested model;
479  * CovMore =  Name of ODS CovParms table for comparison model;
480  %MACRO PseudoR2(NCov=,CovFewer=,CovMore=);
481  DATA &CovFewer.; LENGTH Name $30.; SET &CovFewer.; Name="&CovFewer."; RUN;
482  DATA &CovMore.;  LENGTH Name $30.; SET &CovMore.;  Name="&CovMore.";  RUN;
483  DATA CovCompare; LENGTH Name $30.; SET &CovFewer. &CovMore.; RUN;
484  DATA CovCompare; SET CovCompare;
485       PseudoR2=(LAG&Ncov.(Estimate)-Estimate)/LAG&Ncov.(Estimate); RUN;
486  DATA CovCompare; SET CovCompare;
487       IF CovParm IN("UN(2,1)","UN(3,1)","UN(3,2)",
488               "UN(4,1)","UN(4,2)","UN(4,3)",
489               "UN(5,1)","UN(5,2)","UN(5,3)","UN(5,4)",
490               "UN(6,1)","UN(6,2)","UN(6,3)","UN(6,4)","UN(6,5)") THEN DELETE; RUN;
491  TITLE9 "PseudoR2 (% Reduction) for &CovFewer. vs. &CovMore.";
492  PROC PRINT NOOBS DATA=CovCompare; RUN; TITLE9;
493  %MEND PseudoR2;
494  
495  * To use FitTest macro;
496  * FitFewer = name of infocrit table for nested model;
497  * FitMore  = name of infocrit table for comparison model;
498  %MACRO FitTest(FitFewer, FitMore);
499  DATA &FitFewer.; LENGTH Name $30.; SET &FitFewer.; Name="&FitFewer."; RUN;
500  DATA &FitMore.;  LENGTH Name $30.; SET &FitMore.;  Name="&FitMore.";  RUN;
501  DATA FitCompare; LENGTH Name $30.; SET &FitFewer. &FitMore.; RUN;
502  DATA FitCompare; SET FitCompare; DevDiff=Lag1(Neg2LogLike)-Neg2LogLike;
503       DFdiff=Parms-LAG1(Parms); Pvalue=1-PROBCHI(DevDiff,DFdiff);
504       DROP AICC HQIC CAIC; RUN;
505  TITLE2 "Likelihood Ratio Test for &FitFewer. vs. &FitMore.";
506  PROC PRINT NOOBS DATA=FitCompare; RUN; TITLE2;
507  %MEND FitTest;
